	];

    function filter_get_sort(sortcolumns) {
        var state = pp_get_fragment_state();
        if (state['sort'])
            return state['sort'].split(',');
        else
            return [];
    }
    function filter_get_sort_list(sortcolumns) {
        var sortlist = [];
        var sort = filter_get_sort();
        for (var i = 0; i < sort.length; ++i) {
            var sortitem = sortcolumns[sort[i]];
            if (sortitem)
                sortlist.push(sortitem);
        }
        return sortlist;
    }
    function update_category_sort() {
        var sort = filter_get_sort();
        if (sort.length > 0)
            $('#category_sort_options').val(sort[0]);
        else
            $('#category_sort_options').val('popular');
    }

    var current = null;
    $(document).ready(function() {
        $('.trigger-key-metric-breakdown').on('click', function() {
            r_show_dialog('#key_metric_dialog'); return false;
        });
        var pogo = new ParametricPogoStick('power-supply', '');
        var product_table = $('#paginated_table');
        var x = new FilteredFetchList(
            datafilters,
            '/qapi/product/category/',
            {
                
                category: 'power-supply',
                xslug: '',
                token: 'f9f41f4ed3505f86fe2cfe5443d3a2f7:YPaRGKWfkK9FhO4Eu8oo3xONQyoTiOum9MOKyjsDUjYiITN0SY7UfqFHngGZk1rDWQ4a2xFOfK6uQ4BifT6FsyevMfsYaaceDqYzyvaNyqCWJdCmmUBij0TqkYbF4qUEK2Q6ilplIp79a/sZ75fLqwNqW4Y3TuXqRrEoS5hYcr7RA0B50iVUIJ6ujGvWTLf7uAVOl7SogwIBM3eXDBmdoA==',
                tokev: 'bdcba93d'
            },
            function(result) {
                current = result.data;
                $('#category_content').html(result.html);
                stop_loading_animation();
                pogo.set_low_price(result.lowest_price);
                $('#page_button_row_bot').html(result.paging_row);
                if (result.selection_data !== undefined)
                    pogo.set_selection(result.selection_data);
                var selection_ids = pogo.get_selection_ids();
                for (var i = 0; i < selection_ids.length; ++i) {
                    product_table.find('tr.product-id-' + selection_ids[i] + ' input.px').prop('checked', true);
                }
                if (result.compatibility)
                    $('.pp-filter-count').text(result.count + ' Compatible Products');
                else
                    $('.pp-filter-count').text(result.count + ' Products');
                update_filter_breadcrumbs('div.productList__breadcrumbs', result.breadcrumbs);
                for (var i in current) {
                    var pbdata = current[i];
                    if (pbdata.img)
                        product_table.find('tr.product-id-' + pbdata.id + ' div.td__imageWrapper img').attr('src', pbdata.img);
                    else
                        product_table.find('tr.product-id-' + pbdata.id + ' div.td__imageWrapper img').attr('src', '/static/forever/img/no-image.png');
                }
            },
            function(result) {
                current = {};
                $('#category_content').html('');
                stop_loading_animation();
                pogo.set_low_price(10000);
                if (result && result.error) {
                    $('#page_button_row_bot').html(result.error);
                }
                else {
                    $('#page_button_row_bot').html('');
                }
                $('.pp-filter-count').text('Error Fetching Products');
                update_filter_breadcrumbs('div.productList__breadcrumbs', []);
            }
        );
        register_fetchlist_search(x, '#part_category_search');
        register_fetchlist_sort('#part_category_sort');
        init_paging_scroller('#paginated_table');
        init_filter_breadcrumbs('div.productList__breadcrumbs');

        function update_pricing_preferences() {
            var states = {};
            $('input.merchant_select').each(function(i, e) {
                var merchant_id = parseInt($(e).data('merchant-id'));
                states[merchant_id] = $(e).is(':checked');
            });
            pp_common_ajax_callback('/qapi/pricing/set/',
                {
                    country: 0,
                    use_mir: $('#price_settings_mir').is(':checked') ? 1 : 0,
                    use_all_merchants: $('#price_settings_merchant_all').is(':checked') ? 1 : 0,
                    merchant_data: JSON.stringify({states: states})
                },
                function(data) {
                    if (data.success)
                        x.hashchange();
                    else
                        window.alert(data.error);
                }
            );
        }

        $('input.price_setting').on('change', function(){ update_pricing_preferences(); });
        $('input.merchant_select').on('change', function(){ 
            var none_checked = ($('input.merchant_select:checked').length === 0);
            $('#price_settings_merchant_all').prop('checked', none_checked);
            update_pricing_preferences();
        });
        $('#price_settings_merchant_all').on('click', function() {
            return $(this).is(':checked');
        });
        $('#price_settings_merchant_all').on('change', function() {
            $('input.merchant_select').prop('checked', false);
            update_pricing_preferences();
        });
        $('#category_content').on('click', 'input.px', function() {
            var tr = $(this).closest('tr');
            var pbid = parseInt(tr.data('pb-id'));
            tr.find('input.px').prop('checked', $(this).prop('checked'));
            var data = current[pbid];
            pogo.toggle_selection(data);
            filter_clear_selection();
        });
        $('#select_all').on('click', function() {
            $('input.px').prop('checked', true);
            var datas = [];
            $('input.px1').each(function(i, e) {
                var pbid = parseInt($(this).closest('tr').data('pb-id'));
                var data = current[pbid];
                datas.push(data);
            });
            pogo.set_selection(datas);
            return false;
        });
        
        $("table.productList--detailed").pcpptablesorter({
            cssAsc: 'th--sorted th--sortedAscending',
            cssDesc: 'th--sorted th--sortedDescending',
            cssNone: 'th--unsorted',
            headers: {
                0: { sorter: false },
            },
            sortList: filter_get_sort_list(sortcolumns)
        }).bind('sortEnd', function() {
            var s = '';
            for (var i in this.config.sortList) {
                if (s.length > 0)
                   s += ',';
                for (var k in sortcolumns) {
                    if ((sortcolumns[k][0] == this.config.sortList[i][0]) && (sortcolumns[k][1] == this.config.sortList[i][1])) {
                        s += k;
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
            filter_set_sort(s);
        });
        $('#parametric_add_price_alert_button').on('click', function() {
            r_show_dialog('#price_alert_dialog');
            return false;
        });
        $('#view_partlist').on('click', function() {
            $('#partlist_section').show();
            $(this).hide();
            return false;
        });
        $('#category_sort_options').on('change', function() {
            filter_set_sort($(this).val());
            return false;
        });
        $('#sort_options').on('click', 'a', function() {
            filter_set_sort($(this).attr('data-sort-option'));
            r_hide_off_canvas();
            return false;
        });
        $(window).bind('hashchange', function(e) {
            start_loading_animation();
            x.hashchange();
            update_category_sort();
        });
        $(window).trigger('hashchange');
    });

        </script>
